\newcommand{\flags}[2]{ 
\texttt{#1}\newline \texttt{#2}
}
\newcommand{\flagss}[2]{ 
\texttt{#1}\\ \texttt{#2}
}

\begin{sidewaystable}
%\begin{table}[h]
  \centering
  \begin{tabular}{cccccp{2cm}p{1cm}p{6cm}p{3cm}}
opcode  &  mnmonic  &  bytes  &  cycles  &  adr"-mode  &  function  & flags & logic & example \\ 
0x00  &  BRK  & 1  & 0  &  imp  &  interrupt  \newline  (S)-=:PC,P PC:=(\$FFFE)  & \flags{NVBDIZC}{ --1-1-- } & \begin{lstlisting}
    PC = PC + 1 
    bPoke(SP,PC.h) 
    SP = SP - 1 
    bPoke(SP,PC.l) 
    SP = SP - 1 
    bPoke(SP, (P|\$10) ) 
    SP = SP - 1 
    l = bPeek(\$FFFE) 
    h = bPeek(\$FFFF)<<8 
    PC = h|l              
\end{lstlisting} &  \textbf{\texttt{ BRK  }} \\
 \multicolumn{1}{|c|}{\textbf{Text1}} & & & & & & & & \\
0x01  &  ORA  & 2  & 6  &  izx  &  or with accumulator  \newline  A:=A or {adr}  & \flags{NVBDIZC}{ *----*- } & \begin{lstlisting}
    A = A | M 
    P.N = A.7 
    P.Z = (A==0) ? 1:0  
 
\end{lstlisting} &  \textbf{\texttt{ ORA  (\$A5,X)}} \\
0x05  &  ORA  & 2  & 3  &  zp  &  or with accumulator  \newline  A:=A or {adr}  & \flags{NVBDIZC}{ *----*- } & \begin{lstlisting}
    A = A | M 
    P.N = A.7 
    P.Z = (A==0) ? 1:0  
 
\end{lstlisting} &  \textbf{\texttt{ ORA  \$AB}} \\
  \end{tabular}
  \caption{opcode table}
  \label{tab:opcode}
\end{sidewaystable}
%\end{table}

%opcode  &  mnmonic  &  bytes  &  cycles  &  adr"-mode  &  function  & flags & logic & example \\ 


\draw (0,4) rectangle node (id) {\texttt 0x01}  (1,5) ;
\draw (1,4) rectangle node {\texttt BRK}  (2,5) ;
\draw (2,4) rectangle node {\texttt 1}  (3,5) ;
\draw (3,4) rectangle node {\texttt  imp}  (4,5) ;
\draw (4,4) rectangle node {\flags{NVBDIZC}{ --1-1--}}  (12,5) ;
\draw (0,-1) rectangle node {\textbf{\texttt{ BRK  }}}  (12,0) ;
\draw[very thick] (4,0) rectangle node {%\scriptsize 
%sdfsdfsdf
}  (12,4) ;
\draw (0,2) rectangle node  {\scriptsize interrupt} (4,4)   ;
\draw (0,0) rectangle node  {\scriptsize  (S)-=:PC,P PC:=(\$FFFE)} (4,2)   ;

\node[below right] at (0,5) {\scriptsize op} ;
\node[below right] at (1,5) {\scriptsize name} ;
\node[below right] at (2,5) {\scriptsize cycles} ;
\node[below right] at (3,5) {\scriptsize adrmode} ;
\node[below right] at (4,5) {\scriptsize flags} ;
\node[below right] at (0,0) {\scriptsize Example}  ;
\node[below right] at (4,4) {\scriptsize logic} ;
\node[below right] at (0,4) {\scriptsize description} ;
\node[below right] at (0,2) {\scriptsize function} ;


%\node (logic) at (id) {\texttt 0x00} ;

\node[anchor=north west] (logic) at (4,4) {\begin{lstlisting}
    PC = PC + 1 
    bPoke(SP,PC.h) 
    SP = SP - 1 
    bPoke(SP,PC.l) 
    SP = SP - 1 
    bPoke(SP, (P|\$10) ) 
    SP = SP - 1 
    l = bPeek(\$FFFE) 
    h = bPeek(\$FFFF)<<8 
    PC = h|l              
\end{lstlisting}};

\begin{tikzpicture}\draw[very thick] (4,0) rectangle node {}  (12,4) ;\draw (0,4) rectangle node (id) {\texttt 0x00 }  (1,5) ;\draw (1,4) rectangle node {\texttt  BRK }  (2,5) ;\draw (2,4) rectangle node {\texttt  1 }  (3,5) ;\draw (3,4) rectangle node {\texttt    imp }  (4,5) ;\draw (4,4) rectangle node {\flags{NVBDIZC}{ --1-1-- }}  (12,5) ;\draw (0,-1) rectangle node {\textbf{\texttt{   BRK   }}}  (12,0) ;\draw (0,2) rectangle node  {\scriptsize   interrupt } (4,4)   ;\draw (0,0) rectangle node  {\scriptsize    (S)-=:PC,P PC:=(\$FFFE) } (4,2)   ;\node[below right] at (0,5) {\scriptsize op} ;\node[below right] at (1,5) {\scriptsize name} ;\node[below right] at (2,5) {\scriptsize cycles} ;\node[below right] at (3,5) {\scriptsize adr} ;\node[below right] at (4,5) {\scriptsize flags} ;\node[below right] at (0,0) {\scriptsize example}  ;\node[below right] at (4,4) {\scriptsize logic} ;\node[below right] at (0,4) {\scriptsize description} ;\node[below right] at (0,2) {\scriptsize function} ;\node[anchor=north west] (logic) at (4,4) {\begin{lstlisting}
    PC = PC + 1 
    bPoke(SP,PC.h) 
    SP = SP - 1 
    bPoke(SP,PC.l) 
    SP = SP - 1 
    bPoke(SP, (P|\$10) ) 
    SP = SP - 1 
    l = bPeek(\$FFFE) 
    h = bPeek(\$FFFF)<<8 
    PC = h|l              
 
\end{lstlisting}};\end{tikzpicture}

\end{lstlisting}};\end{tikzpicture}

\begin{tikzpicture}\draw (0,4) rectangle node  {\texttt 0x06   }  (1,5) ;\draw (1,4) rectangle node {\texttt  ASL }  (2,5) ;\draw (2,4) rectangle node {\texttt zp  }  (3,5) ;\draw (3,4) rectangle node[minimum width=2cm, text width=2cm,xshift=1em] { \flagss{NVBDIZC}{*\textendash\textendash\textendash\textendash**} }  (5,5) ; \draw (0,3) rectangle node {ASL \$AB}  (3,4) ;  \draw (3,3) rectangle node  { 2  } (4,4)   ; \draw (4,3) rectangle node  { 5  } (5,4)   ;\draw (0,2) rectangle node {   arithmetic shift left  }  (5,3) ; \draw (0,1) rectangle node {   {adr}:={adr}*2  }  (5,2) ;\draw (0,0) rectangle node {\textbf{\texttt{void cpu\_6502\_ASL\_zp(); }}}  (5,1) ; \node[below right] at (0,5) {\scriptsize op} ;\node[below right] at (1,5) {\scriptsize name} ;\node[below right] at (2,5) {\scriptsize adr} ;\node[below right] at (5,5) {\scriptsize logic} ;\node[below right] at (3,4) {\scriptsize bytes} ; \node[below right] at (4,4) {\scriptsize cycles} ;\node[below right] at (0,4) {\scriptsize example}  ;\node[below right] at (0,1) {\scriptsize c--fct} ;\node[below right] at (0,2) {\scriptsize formal};\node[below right] at (0,3) {\scriptsize description};\draw (5,3.33333) rectangle node {}  (12,5) ; \draw[thick] (5,0) rectangle node {}  (12,3.33333) ; \node[below right] at (5,3.33333) {\scriptsize comment};\node[anchor=north west]  at (5,5) {

    P.C = B.7
    B = (B << 1) & $FE
    P.N = B.7
    P.Z = (B==0) ? 1:0

\end{lstlisting}};\end{tikzpicture}

    SP = SP + 1
    l = bPeek(SP)
    SP = SP + 1
    h = bPeek(SP)<<8
    PC = (h|l) +1

\end{lstlisting}};\end{tikzpicture}

\begin{tikzpicture}\draw (0,4) rectangle node  {\texttt 0x61   }  (1,5) ;\draw (1,4) rectangle node {\texttt  ADC }  (2,5) ;\draw (2,4) rectangle node {\texttt izx  }  (3,5) ;\draw (3,4) rectangle node[minimum width=2cm, text width=2cm,xshift=1em] { \flagss{NVBDIZC}{**\textendash\textendash\textendash**} }  (5,5) ; \draw (0,3) rectangle node {ADC (\$A5,X)}  (3,4) ;  \draw (3,3) rectangle node  { 2  } (4,4)   ; \draw (4,3) rectangle node  { 6  } (5,4)   ;\draw (0,2) rectangle node {   add with carry  }  (5,3) ; \draw (0,1) rectangle node {   A:=A+{adr}  }  (5,2) ;\draw (0,0) rectangle node {\textbf{\texttt{void cpu\_6502\_ADC\_izx(); }}}  (5,1) ; \node[below right] at (0,5) {\scriptsize op} ;\node[below right] at (1,5) {\scriptsize name} ;\node[below right] at (2,5) {\scriptsize adr} ;\node[below right] at (5,5) {\scriptsize logic} ;\node[below right] at (3,4) {\scriptsize bytes} ; \node[below right] at (4,4) {\scriptsize cycles} ;\node[below right] at (0,4) {\scriptsize example}  ;\node[below right] at (0,1) {\scriptsize c--fct} ;\node[below right] at (0,2) {\scriptsize formal};\node[below right] at (0,3) {\scriptsize description};\draw (5,1.33333) rectangle node {}  (12,5) ; \draw[thick] (5,0) rectangle node {}  (12,1.33333) ; \node[below right] at (5,1.33333) {\scriptsize comment};\node[anchor=north west]  at (5,5) {
\begin{lstlisting}
    t = A + M + P.C
    P.V = (A.7!=t.7) ? 1:0
    P.N = A.7
    P.Z = (t==0) ? 1:0
    IF (P.D)
      t = bcd(A) + bcd(M) + P.C
      P.C = (t>99) ? 1:0
    ELSE
      P.C = (t>255) ? 1:0
    A = t & 0xFF

\end{lstlisting}};\end{tikzpicture}

    t = A + M + P.C
    P.V = (A.7!=t.7) ? 1:0

      t = bcd(A) + bcd(M) + P.C

\begin{tikzpicture}\draw (0,4) rectangle node  {\texttt 0x66   }  (1,5) ;\draw (1,4) rectangle node {\texttt  ROR }  (2,5) ;\draw (2,4) rectangle node {\texttt zp  }  (3,5) ;\draw (3,4) rectangle node[minimum width=2cm, text width=2cm,xshift=1em] { \flagss{NVBDIZC}{*\textendash\textendash\textendash\textendash**} }  (5,5) ; \draw (0,3) rectangle node {ROR \$AB}  (3,4) ;  \draw (3,3) rectangle node  { 2  } (4,4)   ; \draw (4,3) rectangle node  { 5  } (5,4)   ;\draw (0,2) rectangle node {   rotate right  }  (5,3) ; \draw (0,1) rectangle node {   {adr}:={adr}/2+C*128  }  (5,2) ;\draw (0,0) rectangle node {\textbf{\texttt{void cpu\_6502\_ROR\_zp(); }}}  (5,1) ; \node[below right] at (0,5) {\scriptsize op} ;\node[below right] at (1,5) {\scriptsize name} ;\node[below right] at (2,5) {\scriptsize adr} ;\node[below right] at (5,5) {\scriptsize logic} ;\node[below right] at (3,4) {\scriptsize bytes} ; \node[below right] at (4,4) {\scriptsize cycles} ;\node[below right] at (0,4) {\scriptsize example}  ;\node[below right] at (0,1) {\scriptsize c--fct} ;\node[below right] at (0,2) {\scriptsize formal};\node[below right] at (0,3) {\scriptsize description};\draw (5,2.66667) rectangle node {}  (12,5) ; \draw[thick] (5,0) rectangle node {}  (12,2.66667) ; \node[below right] at (5,2.66667) {\scriptsize comment};\node[anchor=north west]  at (5,5) {
\begin{lstlisting}
    t = B.0
    B = (B >> 1) & $7F
    B = B | ((P.C) ? $80:$00)
    P.C = t
    P.Z = (B==0) ? 1:0
    P.N = B.7

\end{lstlisting}};\end{tikzpicture}

\begin{tikzpicture}\draw (0,4) rectangle node  {\texttt 0x69   }  (1,5) ;\draw (1,4) rectangle node {\texttt  ADC }  (2,5) ;\draw (2,4) rectangle node {\texttt imm  }  (3,5) ;\draw (3,4) rectangle node[minimum width=2cm, text width=2cm,xshift=1em] { \flagss{NVBDIZC}{**\textendash\textendash\textendash**} }  (5,5) ; \draw (0,3) rectangle node {ADC \#\$AB    }  (3,4) ;  \draw (3,3) rectangle node  { 2  } (4,4)   ; \draw (4,3) rectangle node  { 2  } (5,4)   ;\draw (0,2) rectangle node {   add with carry  }  (5,3) ; \draw (0,1) rectangle node {   A:=A+{adr}  }  (5,2) ;\draw (0,0) rectangle node {\textbf{\texttt{void cpu\_6502\_ADC\_imm(); }}}  (5,1) ; \node[below right] at (0,5) {\scriptsize op} ;\node[below right] at (1,5) {\scriptsize name} ;\node[below right] at (2,5) {\scriptsize adr} ;\node[below right] at (5,5) {\scriptsize logic} ;\node[below right] at (3,4) {\scriptsize bytes} ; \node[below right] at (4,4) {\scriptsize cycles} ;\node[below right] at (0,4) {\scriptsize example}  ;\node[below right] at (0,1) {\scriptsize c--fct} ;\node[below right] at (0,2) {\scriptsize formal};\node[below right] at (0,3) {\scriptsize description};\draw (5,1.33333) rectangle node {}  (12,5) ; \draw[thick] (5,0) rectangle node {}  (12,1.33333) ; \node[below right] at (5,1.33333) {\scriptsize comment};\node[anchor=north west]  at (5,5) {
\begin{lstlisting}
    t = A + M + P.C
    P.V = (A.7!=t.7) ? 1:0
    P.N = A.7
    P.Z = (t==0) ? 1:0
    IF (P.D)
      t = bcd(A) + bcd(M) + P.C
      P.C = (t>99) ? 1:0
    ELSE
      P.C = (t>255) ? 1:0
    A = t & 0xFF

\end{lstlisting}};\end{tikzpicture}

\begin{lstlisting}
    t = A + M + P.C
    P.V = (A.7!=t.7) ? 1:0
    P.N = A.7
    P.Z = (t==0) ? 1:0
    IF (P.D)
      t = bcd(A) + bcd(M) + P.C
      P.C = (t>99) ? 1:0
    ELSE
      P.C = (t>255) ? 1:0
    A = t & 0xFF

\end{lstlisting}};\end{tikzpicture}

\begin{tikzpicture}\draw (0,4) rectangle node  {\texttt 0x7E   }  (1,5) ;\draw (1,4) rectangle node {\texttt  ROR }  (2,5) ;\draw (2,4) rectangle node {\texttt abx  }  (3,5) ;\draw (3,4) rectangle node[minimum width=2cm, text width=2cm,xshift=1em] { \flagss{NVBDIZC}{*\textendash\textendash\textendash\textendash**} }  (5,5) ; \draw (0,3) rectangle node {ROR \$ABCD,X}  (3,4) ;  \draw (3,3) rectangle node  { 3  } (4,4)   ; \draw (4,3) rectangle node  { 7  } (5,4)   ;\draw (0,2) rectangle node {   rotate right  }  (5,3) ; \draw (0,1) rectangle node {   {adr}:={adr}/2+C*128  }  (5,2) ;\draw (0,0) rectangle node {\textbf{\texttt{void cpu\_6502\_ROR\_abx(); }}}  (5,1) ; \node[below right] at (0,5) {\scriptsize op} ;\node[below right] at (1,5) {\scriptsize name} ;\node[below right] at (2,5) {\scriptsize adr} ;\node[below right] at (5,5) {\scriptsize logic} ;\node[below right] at (3,4) {\scriptsize bytes} ; \node[below right] at (4,4) {\scriptsize cycles} ;\node[below right] at (0,4) {\scriptsize example}  ;\node[below right] at (0,1) {\scriptsize c--fct} ;\node[below right] at (0,2) {\scriptsize formal};\node[below right] at (0,3) {\scriptsize description};\draw (5,2.66667) rectangle node {}  (12,5) ; \draw[thick] (5,0) rectangle node {}  (12,2.66667) ; \node[below right] at (5,2.66667) {\scriptsize comment};\node[anchor=north west]  at (5,5) {
\begin{lstlisting}
    t = B.0
    B = (B >> 1) & $7F
    B = B | ((P.C) ? $80:$00)
    P.C = t
    P.Z = (B==0) ? 1:0
    P.N = B.7

\end{lstlisting}};\end{tikzpicture}

\begin{tikzpicture}\draw (0,4) rectangle node  {\texttt 0xE1   }  (1,5) ;\draw (1,4) rectangle node {\texttt  SBC }  (2,5) ;\draw (2,4) rectangle node {\texttt izx  }  (3,5) ;\draw (3,4) rectangle node[minimum width=2cm, text width=2cm,xshift=1em] { \flagss{NVBDIZC}{**\textendash\textendash\textendash**} }  (5,5) ; \draw (0,3) rectangle node {SBC (\$A5,X)}  (3,4) ;  \draw (3,3) rectangle node  { 2  } (4,4)   ; \draw (4,3) rectangle node  { 6  } (5,4)   ;\draw (0,2) rectangle node {   subtract with carry  }  (5,3) ; \draw (0,1) rectangle node {   A:=A-{adr}  }  (5,2) ;\draw (0,0) rectangle node {\textbf{\texttt{void cpu\_6502\_SBC\_izx(); }}}  (5,1) ; \node[below right] at (0,5) {\scriptsize op} ;\node[below right] at (1,5) {\scriptsize name} ;\node[below right] at (2,5) {\scriptsize adr} ;\node[below right] at (5,5) {\scriptsize logic} ;\node[below right] at (3,4) {\scriptsize bytes} ; \node[below right] at (4,4) {\scriptsize cycles} ;\node[below right] at (0,4) {\scriptsize example}  ;\node[below right] at (0,1) {\scriptsize c--fct} ;\node[below right] at (0,2) {\scriptsize formal};\node[below right] at (0,3) {\scriptsize description};\draw (5,1.33333) rectangle node {}  (12,5) ; \draw[thick] (5,0) rectangle node {}  (12,1.33333) ; \node[below right] at (5,1.33333) {\scriptsize comment};\node[anchor=north west]  at (5,5) {
\begin{lstlisting}
    IF (P.D)
      t = bcd(A) - bcd(M) - !P.C
      P.V = (t>99 OR t<0) ? 1:0
    ELSE
      t = A - M - !P.C
      P.V = (t>127 OR t<-128) ? 1:0
    P.C = (t>=0) ? 1:0
    P.N = t.7
    P.Z = (t==0) ? 1:0
    A = t & 0xFF

\end{lstlisting}};\end{tikzpicture}

\begin{tikzpicture}\draw (0,4) rectangle node  {\texttt 0xE9   }  (1,5) ;\draw (1,4) rectangle node {\texttt  SBC }  (2,5) ;\draw (2,4) rectangle node {\texttt imm  }  (3,5) ;\draw (3,4) rectangle node[minimum width=2cm, text width=2cm,xshift=1em] { \flagss{NVBDIZC}{**\textendash\textendash\textendash**} }  (5,5) ; \draw (0,3) rectangle node {SBC \#\$AB    }  (3,4) ;  \draw (3,3) rectangle node  { 2  } (4,4)   ; \draw (4,3) rectangle node  { 2  } (5,4)   ;\draw (0,2) rectangle node {   subtract with carry  }  (5,3) ; \draw (0,1) rectangle node {   A:=A-{adr}  }  (5,2) ;\draw (0,0) rectangle node {\textbf{\texttt{void cpu\_6502\_SBC\_imm(); }}}  (5,1) ; \node[below right] at (0,5) {\scriptsize op} ;\node[below right] at (1,5) {\scriptsize name} ;\node[below right] at (2,5) {\scriptsize adr} ;\node[below right] at (5,5) {\scriptsize logic} ;\node[below right] at (3,4) {\scriptsize bytes} ; \node[below right] at (4,4) {\scriptsize cycles} ;\node[below right] at (0,4) {\scriptsize example}  ;\node[below right] at (0,1) {\scriptsize c--fct} ;\node[below right] at (0,2) {\scriptsize formal};\node[below right] at (0,3) {\scriptsize description};\draw (5,1.33333) rectangle node {}  (12,5) ; \draw[thick] (5,0) rectangle node {}  (12,1.33333) ; \node[below right] at (5,1.33333) {\scriptsize comment};\node[anchor=north west]  at (5,5) {
\begin{lstlisting}
    IF (P.D)
      t = bcd(A) - bcd(M) - !P.C
      P.V = (t>99 OR t<0) ? 1:0
    ELSE
      t = A - M - !P.C
      P.V = (t>127 OR t<-128) ? 1:0
    P.C = (t>=0) ? 1:0
    P.N = t.7
    P.Z = (t==0) ? 1:0
    A = t & 0xFF

\end{lstlisting}};\end{tikzpicture}

\begin{tikzpicture}\draw (0,4) rectangle node  {\texttt 0xFE   }  (1,5) ;\draw (1,4) rectangle node {\texttt  INC }  (2,5) ;\draw (2,4) rectangle node {\texttt abx  }  (3,5) ;\draw (3,4) rectangle node[minimum width=2cm, text width=2cm,xshift=1em] { \flagss{NVBDIZC}{*\textendash\textendash\textendash\textendash*\textendash} }  (5,5) ; \draw (0,3) rectangle node {INC \$ABCD,X}  (3,4) ;  \draw (3,3) rectangle node  { 3  } (4,4)   ; \draw (4,3) rectangle node  { 7  } (5,4)   ;\draw (0,2) rectangle node {   increment  }  (5,3) ; \draw (0,1) rectangle node {   {adr}:={adr}+1  }  (5,2) ;\draw (0,0) rectangle node {\textbf{\texttt{void cpu\_6502\_INC\_abx(); }}}  (5,1) ; \node[below right] at (0,5) {\scriptsize op} ;\node[below right] at (1,5) {\scriptsize name} ;\node[below right] at (2,5) {\scriptsize adr} ;\node[below right] at (5,5) {\scriptsize logic} ;\node[below right] at (3,4) {\scriptsize bytes} ; \node[below right] at (4,4) {\scriptsize cycles} ;\node[below right] at (0,4) {\scriptsize example}  ;\node[below right] at (0,1) {\scriptsize c--fct} ;\node[below right] at (0,2) {\scriptsize formal};\node[below right] at (0,3) {\scriptsize description};\draw (5,3.66667) rectangle node {}  (12,5) ; \draw[thick] (5,0) rectangle node {}  (12,3.66667) ; \node[below right] at (5,3.66667) {\scriptsize comment};\node[anchor=north west]  at (5,5) {
\begin{lstlisting}
    M = (M + 1) & $FF
    P.N = M.7
    P.Z = (M==0) ? 1:0

\end{lstlisting}};\end{tikzpicture}

    bPoke(SP,PC.h) 
    SP = SP - 1 
    bPoke(SP,PC.l) 
    SP = SP - 1 
    bPoke(SP, (P|\$10) ) 
    SP = SP - 1 
    l = bPeek(\$FFFE) 
    h = bPeek(\$FFFF)<<8 
    PC = h|l
